margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Karena akar persamaan kuadrat yang baru adalah&nbsp;<a href=\"https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/pengertian-dan-jenis-jenis-transformasi-geometri\" style=\"color: rgb(34, 153, 169); transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;\">transformasi<\/a>&nbsp;akar persamaan kuadrat yang lama, kita bisa gunakan metode substitusi.<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Apa&nbsp;<em>sih<\/em>&nbsp;maksudnya transformasi? Maksudnya, dua-duanya berubahnya sama gitu. Di sini, kedua akarnya sama-sama 3 kali akar-akar yang lama.<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Biar&nbsp;<em>nggak<\/em>&nbsp;bingung, kita pakai variabel&nbsp;<em>p<\/em>&nbsp;untuk persamaan kuadrat yang baru.<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\"><em>Nah<\/em>, jadinya p = 3x atau kalau kita mau x dalam p, jadinya x = 1\/3 p.<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Langsung&nbsp;<em>aja<\/em>&nbsp;kita substitusiin ya,<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; top: -0.5em;\">2<\/span>&nbsp;+ 5x - 3 = 0<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: center;\">2(1\/3p)<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; top: -0.5em;\">2<\/span>&nbsp;+ 5(1\/3p) - 3 = 0<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: center;\">2\/9p<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; top: -0.5em;\">2<\/span>&nbsp;+ 5\/3p - 3 = 0<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: center;\">kedua ruas kita kalikan dengan 9<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: center;\">2p<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; top: -0.5em;\">2<\/span>&nbsp;+ 15p - 27 = 0<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Sehingga, persamaan kuadrat baru yang akar-akarnya 3 kali persamaan kuadrat 2x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; top: -0.5em;\">2<\/span>&nbsp;+ 5x - 3 = 0 adalah 2p<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; top: -0.5em;\">2<\/span>&nbsp;+ 15p - 27 = 0.<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Kalau mau ditulis lagi dalam x juga&nbsp;<em>nggak<\/em>&nbsp;papa. Jadinya,&nbsp; 2x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; top: -0.5em;\">2<\/span>&nbsp;+ 15x - 27 = 0.<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 600;\">Contoh soal 4<\/span><span style=\"color: rgb(109, 158, 235);\">&nbsp;<\/span><\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Diketahui akar-akar persamaan kuadrat x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; top: -0.5em;\">2<\/span>&nbsp;+ qx + r = 0 adalah x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">1<\/span>&nbsp;dan x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">2<\/span>, dimana x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">1<\/span>&nbsp;&lt; x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">2<\/span>. Tentukan persamaan kuadrat dengan akar x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">1<\/span>&nbsp;+ 2 dan x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">2&nbsp;<\/span>- 2.<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 600;\">Penyelesaian:<\/span><\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\"><em>Nah<\/em>, kalau soalnya kayak gini,&nbsp;<em>nggak<\/em>&nbsp;bisa&nbsp;<em>pake<\/em>&nbsp;metode substitusi tadi. Soalnya, x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">1<\/span>&nbsp;dan x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">2<\/span>&nbsp;berubahnya beda. Ada yang ditambah 2, ada yang dikurangi 2.<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Terus, gimana,&nbsp;<em>dong<\/em>? Tenang.<br><br>Akar-akar persamaan kuadrat x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; top: -0.5em;\">2<\/span>&nbsp;+ 3x -10 = 0 adalah x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">1<\/span>&nbsp;dan x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">2<\/span>. Kita langsung faktorin&nbsp;<em>aja<\/em>&nbsp;persamaan kuadratnya, ya. Jadinya,<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: center;\">x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; top: -0.5em;\">2<\/span>&nbsp;+ 3x -10 = 0<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: center;\">(x-2)(x+5) = 0<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Sehingga, diperoleh akar-akarnya, yaitu x = -5 atau x = 2.<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\"><em>Nah<\/em>, di soal diketahui kalau x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">1<\/span>&nbsp;&lt; x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">2<\/span>. Akar yang lebih kecil yang mana? -5&nbsp;<em>kan<\/em>&nbsp;ya. Jadi, x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">1<\/span>&nbsp;= -5 dan x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">2<\/span>&nbsp;= 2.<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Untuk mencari persamaan kuadrat yang barunya, kita bisa gunakan rumus (x - x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">1<\/span>)(x - x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">2<\/span>) = 0. Karena diketahui di soal kalau akar-akarnya x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">1<\/span>&nbsp;+ 2 dan x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">2&nbsp;<\/span>- 2, berarti:&nbsp;<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: center;\">[x - (x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">1<\/span>&nbsp;+ 2)][x - (x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">2<\/span>&nbsp;- 2)]=0&nbsp;<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Kita substitusi nilai x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">1&nbsp;<\/span>dan x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">2<\/span>&nbsp;yang kita dapatkan barusan, sehingga:<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: center;\">[x - (-5 + 2)][x - (2 - 2)]=0&nbsp;<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: center;\">(x-(-3))(x-0) = 0<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: center;\">(x+3)(x) = 0<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: center;\">kita kali silang<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: center;\">x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; top: -0.5em;\">2&nbsp;<\/span>+ 3x = 0<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Jadi, persamaan kuadrat dengan akar x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">1<\/span>&nbsp;+ 2 dan x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">2&nbsp;<\/span>- 2 adalah x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; top: -0.5em;\">2&nbsp;<\/span>+ 3x = 0.&nbsp;<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\"><br>Oke, contoh soalnya sudah ada empat,&nbsp;<em>nih.&nbsp;<\/em>Bisa&nbsp;<em>dong<\/em>&nbsp;sekarang kalau diminta menyusun persamaan kuadrat.&nbsp;<em>Huehehe<\/em>\u2026<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\"><em>Gengs<\/em>, sadar&nbsp;<em>nggak sih<\/em>, salah satu kunci agar pandai dalam matematika itu adalah banyak mengerjakan latihan soal. Dengan begitu, logika berpikir kamu akan semakin terasah, rumus-rumus yang sering digunakan pun akan melekat di otak kamu dengan sendirinya. Selain itu, kamu juga bisa bertemu dengan berbagai macam variasi soal. Jadi, pemahaman materi kamu akan semakin dalam.&nbsp;<em>Nah<\/em>, kamu bisa&nbsp;<em>lho<\/em>&nbsp;cobain latihan berbagai macam soal di&nbsp;<a href=\"https:\/\/ruangguru.com\/?shortlink=eaff0eb9&amp;pid=blog\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" style=\"color: rgb(34, 153, 169); transition: all 0.3s ease 0s; font-weight: bold;\">ruangbelajar<\/a>. Di sana latihan soalnya lengkap dan ada pembahasannya juga.&nbsp;<em>So<\/em>, tunggu apa lagi? border: 0px; vertical-align: bottom; height: auto; width: 820px; display: block; margin: 0px auto;\"><\/div><div style=\"font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px;\">&nbsp;<\/div><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Ada dua metode untuk menyusun persamaan kuadrat. Metode yang pertama, jika diketahui akar-akar persamaan kuadratnya. Lalu, metode yang kedua, jika diketahui jumlah dan hasil kali dari akar-akar persamaan kuadratnya. Nanti&nbsp;<em>pas<\/em>&nbsp;<em>ngerjain<\/em>&nbsp;soal, kamu pilih&nbsp;<em>deh&nbsp;<\/em>pakai metode yang mana, menyesuaikan dengan yang diketahui di soal.<\/p><h2 style=\"font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 35px; line-height: 1.03; position: relative; padding-bottom: 10px; font-weight: 800; margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(6, 0, 255); font-size: 18px;\">1. Menyusun Persamaan Kuadrat Jika Diketahui Akar-akarnya<\/span><\/h2><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Misalnya, diketahui akar-akar persamaan kuadrat adalah x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">1<\/span>&nbsp;dan x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">2<\/span>. Untuk mendapatkan persamaan kuadratnya, kamu bisa substitusi akar-akar tersebut ke persamaan berikut:<\/p><div style=\"font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px;\"><img src=\"https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hs-fs\/hubfs\/Google%20Drive%20Integration\/Cara%20Menyusun%20Persamaan%20Kuadrat%20%20%7C%20Matematika%20%20Kelas%209-3.jpeg?width=600&amp;name=Cara%20Menyusun%20Persamaan%20Kuadrat%20%20%7C%20Matematika%20%20Kelas%209-3.jpeg\" srcset=\"https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hs-fs\/hubfs\/Google%20Drive%20Integration\/Cara%20Menyusun%20Persamaan%20Kuadrat%20%20%7C%20Matematika%20%20Kelas%209-3.jpeg?width=300&amp;name=Cara%20Menyusun%20Persamaan%20Kuadrat%20%20%7C%20Matematika%20%20Kelas%209-3.jpeg 900w, 1500w, 1800w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 600px) 100vw, 600px\" style=\"max-width: 100%; border: 0px; vertical-align: bottom; height: auto; width: 600px; display: block; margin: 0px auto;\"><\/div><div style=\"font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px;\">&nbsp;<\/div><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Kenapa&nbsp;<em>sih&nbsp;<\/em>harus disubstitusi ke persamaan itu? Kamu masih ingat&nbsp;<em>nggak<\/em>, kalau ingin mendapatkan akar-akar dari suatu persamaan kuadrat, salah satu caranya adalah dengan memfaktorkan persamaan kuadrat tersebut.&nbsp;<em>Nah<\/em>, bentuk persamaan (x - x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">1<\/span>)(x - x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">2<\/span>) = 0 adalah hasil dari pemfaktoran persamaan kuadrat. Kalau kita lakukan sedikit operasi aljabar, kita kali silang persamaan itu, maka akan didapat suatu persamaan kuadrat.<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Oke, supaya lebih paham, perhatikan contoh soal di bawah ini,&nbsp;<em>yuk<\/em>!<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 600;\">Contoh soal 1<\/span><\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Tentukan persamaan kuadrat yang akar-akarnya adalah 3 dan -7.<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 600;\">Penyelesaian:<\/span><\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Diketahui akar-akar persamaan kuadrat adalah 3 dan -7. Berarti, kamu bisa tulis x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">1<\/span>&nbsp;= 3 dan x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">2<\/span>&nbsp;= -7. Kemudian, kedua akar tersebut bisa kamu substitusikan ke persamaan (x - x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">1<\/span>)(x - x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">2<\/span>) = 0, sehingga penyelesaiannya menjadi sebagai berikut:<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: center;\">(x - 3)(x - (-7)) = 0<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: center;\">(x - 3)(x + 7) = 0<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: center;\">x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; top: -0.5em;\">2<\/span>&nbsp;+ 7x - 3x - 21 = 0<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: center;\">x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; top: -0.5em;\">2<\/span>&nbsp;+ 4x - 21 = 0<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\"><em>Jadiii,&nbsp;<\/em>persamaan kuadrat yang akar-akarnya 3 dan -7 adalah x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; top: -0.5em;\">2<\/span>&nbsp;+ 4x - 21 = 0.<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Gimana&nbsp;<em>gengs,&nbsp;<\/em>mudah bukan caranya? Cukup dengan mensubstitusi nilai akar-akarnya dan sedikit melakukan operasi aljabar, kamu sudah bisa mendapatkan persamaan kuadratnya.&nbsp;<em>Yuk<\/em>, kita lanjut ke metode kedua, ya!<\/p><h2 style=\"font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 35px; line-height: 1.03; position: relative; padding-bottom: 10px; font-weight: 800; margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(6, 0, 255);\"><span style=\"font-size: 18px;\">2. Menyusun Persamaan Kuadrat Jika Diketahui Jumlah dan Hasil Kali Akar-akarnya<\/span><\/span><\/h2><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Misalkan, akar-akar suatu persamaan kuadrat adalah x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">1<\/span>&nbsp;dan x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">2<\/span>. Jika yang diketahui pada soal adalah jumlah dan hasil kali akar-akarnya, maka untuk mendapatkan persamaan kuadratnya, kamu bisa gunakan rumus berikut ini:<\/p><div style=\"font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px;\"><img Oke, sekarang, kita perhatikan contoh soal dibawah ini, ya!<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 600;\">Contoh soal 2<\/span><\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Tentukan persaman kuadrat yang akar-akarnya adalah \u03b1 dan \u03b2, serta jumlah dan hasil kali akar-akarnya adalah -1 dan -20.<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 600;\">Penyelesaian:<\/span><\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Diketahui akar-akarnya adalah x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">1<\/span>&nbsp;dan x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">2<\/span>. Kemudian, hasil jumlah akar-akarnya adalah -1, berarti x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">1<\/span>&nbsp;+ x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">2<\/span>&nbsp;= -1. Lalu, hasil kali akar-akarnya adalah -20, berarti x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">1<\/span>&nbsp;. x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">2<\/span>&nbsp;= - 20.&nbsp;<em>Nah<\/em>, kamu bisa langsung substitusi hasil jumlah dan kali akar-akar yang sudah diketahui ke persamaan:<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: center;\">x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; top: -0.5em;\">2<\/span>&nbsp;+ 5x - 3 = 0.<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 600;\">Penyelesaian:<\/span><\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Karena akar persamaan kuadrat yang baru adalah&nbsp;<a href=\"https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/pengertian-dan-jenis-jenis-transformasi-geometri\" style=\"color: rgb(34, 153, 169); transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;\">transformasi<\/a>&nbsp;akar persamaan kuadrat yang lama, kita bisa gunakan metode substitusi.<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Apa&nbsp;<em>sih<\/em>&nbsp;maksudnya transformasi? Maksudnya, dua-duanya berubahnya sama gitu. Di sini, kedua akarnya sama-sama 3 kali akar-akar yang lama.<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Biar&nbsp;<em>nggak<\/em>&nbsp;bingung, kita pakai variabel&nbsp;<em>p<\/em>&nbsp;untuk persamaan kuadrat yang baru.<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\"><em>Nah<\/em>, jadinya p = 3x atau kalau kita mau x dalam p, jadinya x = 1\/3 p.<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Langsung&nbsp;<em>aja<\/em>&nbsp;kita substitusiin ya,<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: center;\">2x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; top: -0.5em;\">2<\/span>&nbsp;+ 5x - 3 = 0<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: center;\">2(1\/3p)<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; top: -0.5em;\">2<\/span>&nbsp;+ 5(1\/3p) - 3 = 0<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: center;\">2\/9p<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; top: -0.5em;\">2<\/span>&nbsp;+ 5\/3p - 3 = 0<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: center;\">kedua ruas kita kalikan dengan 9<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: center;\">2p<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; top: -0.5em;\">2<\/span>&nbsp;+ 15p - 27 = 0<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Sehingga, persamaan kuadrat baru yang akar-akarnya 3 kali persamaan kuadrat 2x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; top: -0.5em;\">2<\/span>&nbsp;+ 5x - 3 = 0 adalah 2p<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; top: -0.5em;\">2<\/span>&nbsp;+ 15p - 27 = 0.<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Kalau mau ditulis lagi dalam x juga&nbsp;<em>nggak<\/em>&nbsp;papa. Jadinya,&nbsp; 2x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; top: -0.5em;\">2<\/span>&nbsp;+ 15x - 27 = 0.<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 600;\">Contoh soal 4<\/span><span style=\"color: rgb(109, 158, 235);\">&nbsp;<\/span><\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Diketahui akar-akar persamaan kuadrat x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; top: -0.5em;\">2<\/span>&nbsp;+ qx + r = 0 adalah x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">1<\/span>&nbsp;dan x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">2<\/span>, dimana x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">1<\/span>&nbsp;&lt; x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">2<\/span>. Tentukan persamaan kuadrat dengan akar x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">1<\/span>&nbsp;+ 2 dan x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">2&nbsp;<\/span>- 2.<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 600;\">Penyelesaian:<\/span><\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\"><em>Nah<\/em>, kalau soalnya kayak gini,&nbsp;<em>nggak<\/em>&nbsp;bisa&nbsp;<em>pake<\/em>&nbsp;metode substitusi tadi. Soalnya, x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">1<\/span>&nbsp;dan x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">2<\/span>&nbsp;berubahnya beda. Ada yang ditambah 2, ada yang dikurangi 2.<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Terus, gimana,&nbsp;<em>dong<\/em>? Tenang.<br><br>Akar-akar persamaan kuadrat x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; top: -0.5em;\">2<\/span>&nbsp;+ 3x -10 = 0 adalah x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">1<\/span>&nbsp;dan x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">2<\/span>. Kita langsung faktorin&nbsp;<em>aja<\/em>&nbsp;persamaan kuadratnya, ya. Jadinya,<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: center;\">x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; top: -0.5em;\">2<\/span>&nbsp;+ 3x -10 = 0<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: center;\">(x-2)(x+5) = 0<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Sehingga, diperoleh akar-akarnya, yaitu x = -5 atau x = 2.<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\"><em>Nah<\/em>, di soal diketahui kalau x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">1<\/span>&nbsp;&lt; x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">2<\/span>. Akar yang lebih kecil yang mana? -5&nbsp;<em>kan<\/em>&nbsp;ya. Jadi, x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">1<\/span>&nbsp;= -5 dan x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">2<\/span>&nbsp;= 2.<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Untuk mencari persamaan kuadrat yang barunya, kita bisa gunakan rumus (x - x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">1<\/span>)(x - x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">2<\/span>) = 0. Karena diketahui di soal kalau akar-akarnya x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">1<\/span>&nbsp;+ 2 dan x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">2&nbsp;<\/span>- 2, berarti:&nbsp;<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: center;\">[x - (x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">1<\/span>&nbsp;+ 2)][x - (x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">2<\/span>&nbsp;- 2)]=0&nbsp;<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Kita substitusi nilai x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">1&nbsp;<\/span>dan x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">2<\/span>&nbsp;yang kita dapatkan barusan, sehingga:<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: center;\">[x - (-5 + 2)][x - (2 - 2)]=0&nbsp;<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: center;\">(x-(-3))(x-0) = 0<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: center;\">(x+3)(x) = 0<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: center;\">kita kali silang<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: center;\">x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; top: -0.5em;\">2&nbsp;<\/span>+ 3x = 0<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Jadi, persamaan kuadrat dengan akar x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">1<\/span>&nbsp;+ 2 dan x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">2&nbsp;<\/span>- 2 adalah x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; top: -0.5em;\">2&nbsp;<\/span>+ 3x = 0.&nbsp;<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\"><br>Oke, contoh soalnya sudah ada empat,&nbsp;<em>nih.&nbsp;<\/em>Bisa&nbsp;<em>dong<\/em>&nbsp;sekarang kalau diminta menyusun persamaan kuadrat.&nbsp;<em>Huehehe<\/em>\u2026<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\"><em>Gengs<\/em>, sadar&nbsp;<em>nggak sih<\/em>, salah satu kunci agar pandai dalam matematika itu adalah banyak mengerjakan latihan soal. Dengan begitu, logika berpikir kamu akan semakin terasah, rumus-rumus yang sering digunakan pun akan melekat di otak kamu dengan sendirinya. Selain itu, kamu juga bisa bertemu dengan berbagai macam variasi soal. Jadi, pemahaman materi kamu akan semakin dalam.&nbsp;<em>Nah<\/em>, kamu bisa&nbsp;<em>lho<\/em>&nbsp;cobain latihan berbagai macam soal di&nbsp;<a href=\"https:\/\/ruangguru.com\/?shortlink=eaff0eb9&amp;pid=blog\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" style=\"color: rgb(34, 153, 169); transition: all 0.3s ease 0s; font-weight: bold;\">ruangbelajar<\/a>. Di sana latihan soalnya lengkap dan ada pembahasannya juga.&nbsp;<em>So<\/em>, tunggu apa lagi? Buruan gabung sekarang juga!<\/p>"}|{"Isi Materi":"<div style=\"font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px;\"><br><\/div><div style=\"font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; border: 0px; vertical-align: bottom; height: auto; width: 820px; display: block; margin: 0px auto;\"><\/div><div style=\"font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px;\">&nbsp;<\/div><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Ada dua metode untuk menyusun persamaan kuadrat. Metode yang pertama, jika diketahui akar-akar persamaan kuadratnya. Lalu, metode yang kedua, jika diketahui jumlah dan hasil kali dari akar-akar persamaan kuadratnya. Nanti&nbsp;<em>pas<\/em>&nbsp;<em>ngerjain<\/em>&nbsp;soal, kamu pilih&nbsp;<em>deh&nbsp;<\/em>pakai metode yang mana, menyesuaikan dengan yang diketahui di soal.<\/p><h2 style=\"font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 35px; line-height: 1.03; position: relative; padding-bottom: 10px; font-weight: 800; margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(6, 0, 255); font-size: 18px;\">1. Menyusun Persamaan Kuadrat Jika Diketahui Akar-akarnya<\/span><\/h2><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Misalnya, diketahui akar-akar persamaan kuadrat adalah x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">1<\/span>&nbsp;dan x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">2<\/span>. Untuk mendapatkan persamaan kuadratnya, kamu bisa substitusi akar-akar tersebut ke persamaan berikut:<\/p><div style=\"font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px;\"><img src=\"https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hs-fs\/hubfs\/Google%20Drive%20Integration\/Cara%20Menyusun%20Persamaan%20Kuadrat%20%20%7C%20Matematika%20%20Kelas%209-3.jpeg?width=600&amp;name=Cara%20Menyusun%20Persamaan%20Kuadrat%20%20%7C%20Matematika%20%20Kelas%209-3.jpeg\" srcset=\"https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hs-fs\/hubfs\/Google%20Drive%20Integration\/Cara%20Menyusun%20Persamaan%20Kuadrat%20%20%7C%20Matematika%20%20Kelas%209-3.jpeg?width=300&amp;name=Cara%20Menyusun%20Persamaan%20Kuadrat%20%20%7C%20Matematika%20%20Kelas%209-3.jpeg 1500w, 1800w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 600px) 100vw, 600px\" style=\"max-width: 100%; border: 0px; vertical-align: bottom; height: auto; width: 600px; display: block; margin: 0px auto;\"><\/div><div style=\"font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px;\">&nbsp;<\/div><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Kenapa&nbsp;<em>sih&nbsp;<\/em>harus disubstitusi ke persamaan itu? Kamu masih ingat&nbsp;<em>nggak<\/em>, kalau ingin mendapatkan akar-akar dari suatu persamaan kuadrat, salah satu caranya adalah dengan memfaktorkan persamaan kuadrat tersebut.&nbsp;<em>Nah<\/em>, bentuk persamaan (x - x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">1<\/span>)(x - x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">2<\/span>) = 0 adalah hasil dari pemfaktoran persamaan kuadrat. Kalau kita lakukan sedikit operasi aljabar, kita kali silang persamaan itu, maka akan didapat suatu persamaan kuadrat.<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Oke, supaya lebih paham, perhatikan contoh soal di bawah ini,&nbsp;<em>yuk<\/em>!<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 600;\">Contoh soal 1<\/span><\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Tentukan persamaan kuadrat yang akar-akarnya adalah 3 dan -7.<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 600;\">Penyelesaian:<\/span><\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Diketahui akar-akar persamaan kuadrat adalah 3 dan -7. Berarti, kamu bisa tulis x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">1<\/span>&nbsp;= 3 dan x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">2<\/span>&nbsp;= -7. Kemudian, kedua akar tersebut bisa kamu substitusikan ke persamaan (x - x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">1<\/span>)(x - x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">2<\/span>) = 0, sehingga penyelesaiannya menjadi sebagai berikut:<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: center;\">(x - 3)(x - (-7)) = 0<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: center;\">(x - 3)(x + 7) = 0<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: center;\">x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; top: -0.5em;\">2<\/span>&nbsp;+ 7x - 3x - 21 = 0<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: center;\">x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; top: -0.5em;\">2<\/span>&nbsp;+ 4x - 21 = 0<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\"><em>Jadiii,&nbsp;<\/em>persamaan kuadrat yang akar-akarnya 3 dan -7 adalah x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; top: -0.5em;\">2<\/span>&nbsp;+ 4x - 21 = 0.<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Gimana&nbsp;<em>gengs,&nbsp;<\/em>mudah bukan caranya? Cukup dengan mensubstitusi nilai akar-akarnya dan sedikit melakukan operasi aljabar, kamu sudah bisa mendapatkan persamaan kuadratnya.&nbsp;<em>Yuk<\/em>, kita lanjut ke metode kedua, ya!<\/p><h2 style=\"font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 35px; line-height: 1.03; position: relative; padding-bottom: 10px; font-weight: 800; margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(6, 0, 255);\"><span style=\"font-size: 18px;\">2. Menyusun Persamaan Kuadrat Jika Diketahui Jumlah dan Hasil Kali Akar-akarnya<\/span><\/span><\/h2><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Misalkan, akar-akar suatu persamaan kuadrat adalah x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">1<\/span>&nbsp;dan x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">2<\/span>. Jika yang diketahui pada soal adalah jumlah dan hasil kali akar-akarnya, maka untuk mendapatkan persamaan kuadratnya, kamu bisa gunakan rumus berikut ini:<\/p><div style=\"font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px;\"><img Oke, sekarang, kita perhatikan contoh soal dibawah ini, ya!<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 600;\">Contoh soal 2<\/span><\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Tentukan persaman kuadrat yang akar-akarnya adalah \u03b1 dan \u03b2, serta jumlah dan hasil kali akar-akarnya adalah -1 dan -20.<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 600;\">Penyelesaian:<\/span><\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Diketahui akar-akarnya adalah x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">1<\/span>&nbsp;dan x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">2<\/span>. Kemudian, hasil jumlah akar-akarnya adalah -1, berarti x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">1<\/span>&nbsp;+ x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">2<\/span>&nbsp;= -1. Lalu, hasil kali akar-akarnya adalah -20, berarti x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">1<\/span>&nbsp;. x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">2<\/span>&nbsp;= - 20.&nbsp;<em>Nah<\/em>, kamu bisa langsung substitusi hasil jumlah dan kali akar-akar yang sudah diketahui ke persamaan:<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: center;\">x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; top: -0.5em;\">2<\/span>&nbsp;+ 5x - 3 = 0.<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 600;\">Penyelesaian:<\/span><\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Karena akar persamaan kuadrat yang baru adalah&nbsp;<a href=\"https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/pengertian-dan-jenis-jenis-transformasi-geometri\" style=\"color: rgb(34, 153, 169); transition: all 0.3s ease 0s;\">transformasi<\/a>&nbsp;akar persamaan kuadrat yang lama, kita bisa gunakan metode substitusi.<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Apa&nbsp;<em>sih<\/em>&nbsp;maksudnya transformasi? Maksudnya, dua-duanya berubahnya sama gitu. Di sini, kedua akarnya sama-sama 3 kali akar-akar yang lama.<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Biar&nbsp;<em>nggak<\/em>&nbsp;bingung, kita pakai variabel&nbsp;<em>p<\/em>&nbsp;untuk persamaan kuadrat yang baru.<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\"><em>Nah<\/em>, jadinya p = 3x atau kalau kita mau x dalam p, jadinya x = 1\/3 p.<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Langsung&nbsp;<em>aja<\/em>&nbsp;kita substitusiin ya,<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: center;\">2x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; top: -0.5em;\">2<\/span>&nbsp;+ 5x - 3 = 0<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: center;\">2(1\/3p)<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; top: -0.5em;\">2<\/span>&nbsp;+ 5(1\/3p) - 3 = 0<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: center;\">2\/9p<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; top: -0.5em;\">2<\/span>&nbsp;+ 5\/3p - 3 = 0<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: center;\">kedua ruas kita kalikan dengan 9<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: center;\">2p<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; top: -0.5em;\">2<\/span>&nbsp;+ 15p - 27 = 0<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Sehingga, persamaan kuadrat baru yang akar-akarnya 3 kali persamaan kuadrat 2x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; top: -0.5em;\">2<\/span>&nbsp;+ 5x - 3 = 0 adalah 2p<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; top: -0.5em;\">2<\/span>&nbsp;+ 15p - 27 = 0.<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Kalau mau ditulis lagi dalam x juga&nbsp;<em>nggak<\/em>&nbsp;papa. Jadinya,&nbsp; 2x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; top: -0.5em;\">2<\/span>&nbsp;+ 15x - 27 = 0.<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 600;\">Contoh soal 4<\/span><span style=\"color: rgb(109, 158, 235);\">&nbsp;<\/span><\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Diketahui akar-akar persamaan kuadrat x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; top: -0.5em;\">2<\/span>&nbsp;+ qx + r = 0 adalah x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">1<\/span>&nbsp;dan x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">2<\/span>, dimana x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">1<\/span>&nbsp;&lt; x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">2<\/span>. Tentukan persamaan kuadrat dengan akar x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">1<\/span>&nbsp;+ 2 dan x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">2&nbsp;<\/span>- 2.<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 600;\">Penyelesaian:<\/span><\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\"><em>Nah<\/em>, kalau soalnya kayak gini,&nbsp;<em>nggak<\/em>&nbsp;bisa&nbsp;<em>pake<\/em>&nbsp;metode substitusi tadi. Soalnya, x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">1<\/span>&nbsp;dan x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">2<\/span>&nbsp;berubahnya beda. Ada yang ditambah 2, ada yang dikurangi 2.<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Terus, gimana,&nbsp;<em>dong<\/em>? Tenang.<br><br>Akar-akar persamaan kuadrat x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; top: -0.5em;\">2<\/span>&nbsp;+ 3x -10 = 0 adalah x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">1<\/span>&nbsp;dan x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">2<\/span>. Kita langsung faktorin&nbsp;<em>aja<\/em>&nbsp;persamaan kuadratnya, ya. Jadinya,<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: center;\">x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; top: -0.5em;\">2<\/span>&nbsp;+ 3x -10 = 0<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: center;\">(x-2)(x+5) = 0<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Sehingga, diperoleh akar-akarnya, yaitu x = -5 atau x = 2.<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\"><em>Nah<\/em>, di soal diketahui kalau x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">1<\/span>&nbsp;&lt; x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">2<\/span>. Akar yang lebih kecil yang mana? -5&nbsp;<em>kan<\/em>&nbsp;ya. Jadi, x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">1<\/span>&nbsp;= -5 dan x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">2<\/span>&nbsp;= 2.<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Untuk mencari persamaan kuadrat yang barunya, kita bisa gunakan rumus (x - x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">1<\/span>)(x - x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">2<\/span>) = 0. Karena diketahui di soal kalau akar-akarnya x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">1<\/span>&nbsp;+ 2 dan x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">2&nbsp;<\/span>- 2, berarti:&nbsp;<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: center;\">[x - (x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">1<\/span>&nbsp;+ 2)][x - (x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">2<\/span>&nbsp;- 2)]=0&nbsp;<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Kita substitusi nilai x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">1&nbsp;<\/span>dan x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">2<\/span>&nbsp;yang kita dapatkan barusan, sehingga:<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: center;\">[x - (-5 + 2)][x - (2 - 2)]=0&nbsp;<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: center;\">(x-(-3))(x-0) = 0<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: center;\">(x+3)(x) = 0<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: center;\">kita kali silang<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: center;\">x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; top: -0.5em;\">2&nbsp;<\/span>+ 3x = 0<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Jadi, persamaan kuadrat dengan akar x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">1<\/span>&nbsp;+ 2 dan x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">2&nbsp;<\/span>- 2 adalah x<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; top: -0.5em;\">2&nbsp;<\/span>+ 3x = 0.&nbsp;<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\"><br>Oke, contoh soalnya sudah ada empat,&nbsp;<em>nih.&nbsp;<\/em>Bisa&nbsp;<em>dong<\/em>&nbsp;sekarang kalau diminta menyusun persamaan kuadrat.&nbsp;<em>Huehehe<\/em>\u2026<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\"><em>Gengs<\/em>, sadar&nbsp;<em>nggak sih<\/em>, salah satu kunci agar pandai dalam matematika itu adalah banyak mengerjakan latihan soal. Dengan begitu, logika berpikir kamu akan semakin terasah, rumus-rumus yang sering digunakan pun akan melekat di otak kamu dengan sendirinya. Selain itu, kamu juga bisa bertemu dengan berbagai macam variasi soal. Jadi, pemahaman materi kamu akan semakin dalam.&nbsp;<em>Nah<\/em>, kamu bisa&nbsp;<em>lho<\/em>&nbsp;cobain latihan berbagai macam soal di&nbsp;<a href=\"https:\/\/ruangguru.com\/?shortlink=eaff0eb9&amp;pid=blog\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" style=\"color: rgb(34, 153, 169); transition: all 0.3s ease 0s; font-weight: bold;\">ruangbelajar<\/a>. Di sana latihan soalnya lengkap dan ada pembahasannya juga.&nbsp;<em>So<\/em>, tunggu apa lagi? Buruan gabung sekarang juga!<\/p>"}|Success to update materi with materi title Cara menyusun persamaan kuadrat|Update|2020-12-14 11:52:00|#|4|Teachers|teacher|Materi|{"Judul Materi":"Determinan dan Invers Matriks","Mapel Materi":"Matematika","Materi Untuk Kelas":"XI","Isi Materi":"<p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px;\"><img src=\"https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hs-fs\/hubfs\/separator-06.png?width=820&amp;name=separator-06.png\" alt=\"determinan matriks\" width=\"820\" srcset=\"https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hs-fs\/hubfs\/separator-06.png?width=410&amp;name=separator-06.png 410w, https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hs-fs\/hubfs\/separator-06.png?width=820&amp;name=separator-06.png 820w, https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hs-fs\/hubfs\/separator-06.png?width=1230&amp;name=separator-06.png 1230w, https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hs-fs\/hubfs\/separator-06.png?width=1640&amp;name=separator-06.png 1640w, https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hs-fs\/hubfs\/separator-06.png?width=2050&amp;name=separator-06.png 2050w, https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hs-fs\/hubfs\/separator-06.png?width=2460&amp;name=separator-06.png 2460w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 820px) 100vw, 820px\" style=\"max-width: 100%; border: 0px; vertical-align: bottom; height: auto; width: 820px; display: block; margin: 0px auto;\"><\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\"><em>Well<\/em>, kita mulai dari determinan matriks terlebih dahulu, ya. Kenapa? Soalnya, untuk mencari invers suatu matriks, kita perlu mencari determinannya lebih dulu. Teman-teman ada yang&nbsp;<em>udah tau<\/em>&nbsp;apa itu determinan matriks?&nbsp;<span style=\"font-weight: 600;\">Determinan adalah nilai yang dapat dihitung dari unsur-unsur suatu matriks persegi<\/span>. Maksudnya matriks persegi tuh yang kayak gimana sih? Matriks persegi adalah matriks yang memiliki jumlah baris dan kolom yang sama, sehingga kalau kita gambarkan bentuk matriksnya, akan membentuk bangun layaknya persegi.<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px;\">\u201cJadi, kalau jumlah baris dan kolomnya&nbsp;<em>nggak<\/em>&nbsp;sama, kita&nbsp;<em>nggak<\/em>&nbsp;bisa mencari determinannya?\u201d<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px;\">Jawabannya&nbsp;<em>udah<\/em>&nbsp;pasti,<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px;\"><img src=\"https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hs-fs\/hubfs\/ezgif.com-resize.gif?width=300&amp;name=ezgif.com-resize.gif\" alt=\"yes\" width=\"300\" srcset=\"https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hs-fs\/hubfs\/ezgif.com-resize.gif?width=150&amp;name=ezgif.com-resize.gif 150w, https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hs-fs\/hubfs\/ezgif.com-resize.gif?width=300&amp;name=ezgif.com-resize.gif 300w, https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hs-fs\/hubfs\/ezgif.com-resize.gif?width=450&amp;name=ezgif.com-resize.gif 450w, https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hs-fs\/hubfs\/ezgif.com-resize.gif?width=600&amp;name=ezgif.com-resize.gif 600w, https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hs-fs\/hubfs\/ezgif.com-resize.gif?width=750&amp;name=ezgif.com-resize.gif 750w, https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hs-fs\/hubfs\/ezgif.com-resize.gif?width=900&amp;name=ezgif.com-resize.gif 900w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 300px) 100vw, 300px\" style=\"max-width: 100%; font-size: 16px; text-align: center;\">(sumber: giphy.com)<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Gimana, paham ya sampai sini? Oke, kita lanjut, ya. Misalnya, terdapat suatu matriks yang kita beri nama matriks A. Determinan matriks A bisa ditulis dengan tanda&nbsp;<span style=\"font-weight: 600;\">det (A), det A, atau |A|<\/span>. Nah, cara mencari determinan suatu matriks juga berbeda-beda, tergantung dari ordonya. Kita bahas satu-satu, ya...<\/p><h2 style=\"font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 20px; line-height: 1.03; position: relative; padding-bottom: 10px; font-weight: 800; margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);\"><span style=\"color: rgb(6, 0, 255);\">a. Determinan Matriks Ordo 2x2<\/span><\/h2><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Misalkan,<img src=\"https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hs-fs\/hubfs\/determinan1.png?width=100&amp;name=determinan1.png\" alt=\"determinan\" width=\"100\" srcset=\"https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hs-fs\/hubfs\/determinan1.png?width=50&amp;name=determinan1.png 50w, https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hs-fs\/hubfs\/determinan1.png?width=100&amp;name=determinan1.png 100w, https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hs-fs\/hubfs\/determinan1.png?width=150&amp;name=determinan1.png 150w, https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hs-fs\/hubfs\/determinan1.png?width=200&amp;name=determinan1.png 200w, https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hs-fs\/hubfs\/determinan1.png?width=250&amp;name=determinan1.png 250w, https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hs-fs\/hubfs\/determinan1.png?width=300&amp;name=determinan1.png 300w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 100px) 100vw, 100px\" style=\"max-width: 100%; border: 0px; vertical-align: bottom; height: auto; width: 100px;\">adalah matriks berordo 2x2. Elemen a dan d terletak pada diagonal utama, sedangkan elemen b dan c terletak pada diagonal kedua. Determinan matriks A dapat diperoleh dengan mengurangkan hasil kali elemen-elemen diagonal utama dengan hasil kali elemen-elemen diagonal kedua.<\/p><div style=\"font-family: &quot;Source Sans ternyata.&nbsp;<em>Hm<\/em>, kira-kira, mencari determinan matriks berordo 3x3 mudah juga&nbsp;<em>nggak<\/em>&nbsp;ya? Yuk, kita cari&nbsp;<em>tau<\/em>!<\/p><h2 style=\"font-family: &quot;Open Sans&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 20px; line-height: 1.03; position: relative; padding-bottom: 10px; font-weight: 800; margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);\"><span style=\"color: rgb(6, 0, 255);\">b. Determinan Matriks Ordo 3x3<\/span><\/h2><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Misalkan,<img src=\"https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hs-fs\/hubfs\/determinan4.png?width=110&amp;name=determinan4.png\" alt=\"determinan\" width=\"110\" srcset=\"https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hs-fs\/hubfs\/determinan4.png?width=55&amp;name=determinan4.png 55w, https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hs-fs\/hubfs\/determinan4.png?width=110&amp;name=determinan4.png 110w, https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hs-fs\/hubfs\/determinan4.png?width=165&amp;name=determinan4.png 165w, https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hs-fs\/hubfs\/determinan4.png?width=220&amp;name=determinan4.png 220w, https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hs-fs\/hubfs\/determinan4.png?width=275&amp;name=determinan4.png 275w, https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hs-fs\/hubfs\/determinan4.png?width=330&amp;name=determinan4.png 330w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 110px) 100vw, 110px\" style=\"max-width: 100%; border: 0px; vertical-align: bottom; height: auto; width: 110px;\">adalah matriks berordo 3x3. Terdapat dua cara yang bisa dilakukan untuk mencari determinannya, yaitu menggunakan aturan&nbsp;<em>Sarrus<\/em>&nbsp;dan metode minor-kofaktor.<\/p><div style=\"font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px;\"><img src=\"https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hs-fs\/hubfs\/Matematika_Matriks-03.png?width=600&amp;name=Matematika_Matriks-03.png\" alt=\"determinan matriks ordo 3x3\" width=\"600\" srcset=\"https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hs-fs\/hubfs\/Matematika_Matriks-03.png?width=300&amp;name=Matematika_Matriks-03.png 300w, https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hs-fs\/hubfs\/Matematika_Matriks-03.png?width=600&amp;name=Matematika_Matriks-03.png 600w, https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hs-fs\/hubfs\/Matematika_Matriks-03.png?width=900&amp;name=Matematika_Matriks-03.png 900w, https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hs-fs\/hubfs\/Matematika_Matriks-03.png?width=1200&amp;name=Matematika_Matriks-03.png 1200w, https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hs-fs\/hubfs\/Matematika_Matriks-03.png?width=1500&amp;name=Matematika_Matriks-03.png 1500w, https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hs-fs\/hubfs\/Matematika_Matriks-03.png?width=1800&amp;name=Matematika_Matriks-03.png 1800w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 600px) 100vw, 600px\" style=\"max-width: 100%; border: 0px; vertical-align: bottom; height: auto; width: 600px; display: block; margin: 0px auto;\"><\/div><div style=\"font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px;\">&nbsp;<\/div><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\"><em>Hmm<\/em>\u2026 Kamu pasti bingung ya maksud rumus di atas. Tenang&nbsp;<em>aja<\/em>, di bawah ini&nbsp;<em>udah<\/em>&nbsp;ada contoh soal dan pembahasannya kok. Jadi, bisa kamu pahami dengan baik. Tapi, jangan cuma dibaca&nbsp;<em>aja<\/em>&nbsp;ya. Supaya kamu lebih mudah paham, coba deh ikutan corat-coret di kertas.&nbsp;<em>Yuk<\/em>, siapkan pulpen dan kertasnya!<\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 600;\">Contoh soal<\/span><\/p><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px;\">Tentukan determinan matriks berikut ini menggunakan aturan&nbsp;<em>Sarrus<\/em>&nbsp;dan metode minor-kofaktor!<\/p><div style=\"font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px;\"><img src=\"https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hubfs\/Matematika%20Kelas%2011%20%7C%20Cara%20Mencari%20Determinan%20dan%20Invers%20Matriks-9.png\" alt=\"\" style=\"max-width: 100%; border: 0px; vertical-align: bottom; height: auto; display: block; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;\"><\/div><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 600;\">Pembahasan:<\/span><\/p><ul style=\"font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px;\"><li><span style=\"font-weight: 600;\">Aturan&nbsp;<em>Sarrus<\/em><\/span><\/li><\/ul><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Agar lebih mudah, kita tulis kembali elemen-elemen pada kolom ke-1 dan ke-2 di sebelah kanan matriks A sebagai berikut:<\/p><div style=\"font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px;\"><img src=\"https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hs-fs\/hubfs\/determinan6.png?width=231&amp;name=determinan6.png\" alt=\"determinan\" width=\"231\" srcset=\"https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hs-fs\/hubfs\/determinan6.png?width=116&amp;name=determinan6.png 116w, https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hs-fs\/hubfs\/determinan6.png?width=231&amp;name=determinan6.png 231w, https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hs-fs\/hubfs\/determinan6.png?width=347&amp;name=determinan6.png 347w, https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hs-fs\/hubfs\/determinan6.png?width=462&amp;name=determinan6.png 462w, https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hs-fs\/hubfs\/determinan6.png?width=578&amp;name=determinan6.png 578w, https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hs-fs\/hubfs\/determinan6.png?width=693&amp;name=determinan6.png 693w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 231px) 100vw, 231px\" style=\"max-width: 100%; border: 0px; vertical-align: bottom; height: auto; width: 231px; display: block; margin: 0px auto;\"><\/div><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Kemudian, kita tarik garis putus-putus seperti gambar di atas. Kalikan elemen-elemen yang terkena garis putus-putus tersebut. Hasil kali elemen yang terkena garis putus-putus berwarna biru diberi tanda positif (+), sedangkan hasil kali elemen yang terkena garis putus-putus berwarna oranye diberi tanda negatif (-). Ingat urutan penulisannya juga, ya!<\/p><div style=\"font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px;\"><img src=\"https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hubfs\/Matematika%20Kelas%2011%20%7C%20Cara%20Mencari%20Determinan%20dan%20Invers%20Matriks-12.png\" alt=\"\" style=\"max-width: 100%; border: 0px; vertical-align: bottom; height: auto; display: block; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;\"><\/div><div style=\"font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px;\">&nbsp;<\/div><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Sepintas terlihat cukup rumit ya. Tapi, kalau kamu sering berlatih soal, pasti akan hafal dengan sendirinya. Jadi, jangan malas untuk berlatih soal, ya! Sekarang, kita coba kerjakan menggunakan metode yang satunya lagi&nbsp;<em>kuy<\/em>!<\/p><ul style=\"font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px;\"><li><span style=\"font-weight: 600;\">Metode Minor-Kofaktor<\/span><\/li><\/ul><p style=\"margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 0px; font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Berdasarkan rumus minor-kofaktor di atas, determinan matriks A dapat dicari dengan menghitung jumlah seluruh hasil kali antara kofaktor matriks bagian dari matriks A dengan elemen-elemen pada salah satu baris atau kolom matriks A. Jadi, pertama, kita pilih salah satu baris atau kolom matriks A untuk mendapatkan nilai determinannya. Misalnya, kita pilih baris ke-1. Elemen-elemen matriks baris ke-1, yaitu a<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">11<\/span>, a<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">12<\/span>, dan a<span style=\"position: relative; font-size: 12px; line-height: 0; vertical-align: baseline; bottom: -0.25em;\">13<\/span>.<\/p><div style=\"font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px;\"><img src=\"https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hs-fs\/hubfs\/Matematika%20Kelas%2011%20%7C%20Cara%20Mencari%20Determinan%20dan%20Invers%20Matriks-19.png?width=137&amp;name=Matematika%20Kelas%2011%20%7C%20Cara%20Mencari%20Determinan%20dan%20Invers%20Matriks-19.png\" width=\"137\" alt=\"determinan\" srcset=\"https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hs-fs\/hubfs\/Matematika%20Kelas%2011%20%7C%20Cara%20Mencari%20Determinan%20dan%20Invers%20Matriks-19.png?width=69&amp;name=Matematika%20Kelas%2011%20%7C%20Cara%20Mencari%20Determinan%20dan%20Invers%20Matriks-19.png 69w, https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hs-fs\/hubfs\/Matematika%20Kelas%2011%20%7C%20Cara%20Mencari%20Determinan%20dan%20Invers%20Matriks-19.png?width=137&amp;name=Matematika%20Kelas%2011%20%7C%20Cara%20Mencari%20Determinan%20dan%20Invers%20Matriks-19.png 137w, https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hs-fs\/hubfs\/Matematika%20Kelas%2011%20%7C%20Cara%20Mencari%20Determinan%20dan%20Invers%20Matriks-19.png?width=206&amp;name=Matematika%20Kelas%2011%20%7C%20Cara%20Mencari%20Determinan%20dan%20Invers%20Matriks-19.png 206w, https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hs-fs\/hubfs\/Matematika%20Kelas%2011%20%7C%20Cara%20Mencari%20Determinan%20dan%20Invers%20Matriks-19.png?width=274&amp;name=Matematika%20Kelas%2011%20%7C%20Cara%20Mencari%20Determinan%20dan%20Invers%20Matriks-19.png 274w, https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hs-fs\/hubfs\/Matematika%20Kelas%2011%20%7C%20Cara%20Mencari%20Determinan%20dan%20Invers%20Matriks-19.png?width=343&amp;name=Matematika%20Kelas%2011%20%7C%20Cara%20Mencari%20Determinan%20dan%20Invers%20Matriks-19.png 343w, https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hs-fs\/hubfs\/Matematika%20Kelas%2011%20%7C%20Cara%20Mencari%20Determinan%20dan%20Invers%20Matriks-19.png?width=411&amp;name=Matematika%20Kelas%2011%20%7C%20Cara%20Mencari%20Determinan%20dan%20Invers%20Matriks-19.png 411w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 137px) 100vw, 137px\" style=\"max-width: 100%; font-size: 16px; text-align: justify;\">Selanjutnya, karena kita pilih elemen-elemen pada baris ke-1, rumus determinan matriks yang kita gunakan adalah sebagai berikut:<\/p><div style=\"font-family: &quot;Source Sans Pro&quot;, sans-serif; font-size: 16px;\"><img src=\"https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hs-fs\/hubfs\/Matematika%20Kelas%2011%20%7C%20Cara%20Mencari%20Determinan%20dan%20Invers%20Matriks-14.png?width=439&amp;name=Matematika%20Kelas%2011%20%7C%20Cara%20Mencari%20Determinan%20dan%20Invers%20Matriks-14.png\" alt=\"determinan\" width=\"439\" srcset=\"https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hs-fs\/hubfs\/Matematika%20Kelas%2011%20%7C%20Cara%20Mencari%20Determinan%20dan%20Invers%20Matriks-14.png?width=220&amp;name=Matematika%20Kelas%2011%20%7C%20Cara%20Mencari%20Determinan%20dan%20Invers%20Matriks-14.png 220w, https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hs-fs\/hubfs\/Matematika%20Kelas%2011%20%7C%20Cara%20Mencari%20Determinan%20dan%20Invers%20Matriks-14.png?width=439&amp;name=Matematika%20Kelas%2011%20%7C%20Cara%20Mencari%20Determinan%20dan%20Invers%20Matriks-14.png 439w, https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hs-fs\/hubfs\/Matematika%20Kelas%2011%20%7C%20Cara%20Mencari%20Determinan%20dan%20Invers%20Matriks-14.png?width=659&amp;name=Matematika%20Kelas%2011%20%7C%20Cara%20Mencari%20Determinan%20dan%20Invers%20Matriks-14.png 659w, https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hs-fs\/hubfs\/Matematika%20Kelas%2011%20%7C%20Cara%20Mencari%20Determinan%20dan%20Invers%20Matriks-14.png?width=878&amp;name=Matematika%20Kelas%2011%20%7C%20Cara%20Mencari%20Determinan%20dan%20Invers%20Matriks-14.png 878w, https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hs-fs\/hubfs\/Matematika%20Kelas%2011%20%7C%20Cara%20Mencari%20Determinan%20dan%20Invers%20Matriks-14.png?width=1098&amp;name=Matematika%20Kelas%2011%20%7C%20Cara%20Mencari%20Determinan%20dan%20Invers%20Matriks-14.png 1098w, https:\/\/blog.ruangguru.com\/hs-fs\/hubfs\/Matematika%20Kelas%2011%20%7C%20Cara%20Mencari%20Determinan%20dan%20Invers%20Matriks-14.png?width=1317&amp;name=Matematika%20Kelas%2011%20%7C%20Cara%20Mencari%20Determinan%20dan%20Invers%20Matriks-14.png 1317w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 439px) 100vw, 439px\" style=\"max-width: 100%;
